ASSAY_NOTE	Data from Supporting Information Table S2. The mean concentrations (ng/mL), standard deviation, range, and number of samples with concentration of PFCA and diPAP from Münster and Halle.
ASSAY_NOTE	Halle (150 samples); 10 samples per year were analyzed from 1995 to 2009 (except 2006, n = 11)
ASSAY_NOTE	22 PFASs analyzed, 14 of which reported here; 8 reported in Part II
ASSAY_NOTE	N for specific year/sex combination not preserved here
ASSAY_NOTE	human plasma samples archived by the German Environmental Specimen Bank (GSB)

DATA_COLLECTION	Germany GSB PFAS II Plasma 1982-2009
ASSAY_NAME	PFAS in plasma from 2 German Cities 1982-2009 (II)
ASSAY_DESCRIPTION	Temporal Study of certain PFAS in archived human plasma from two German cities 1982 – 2009; Part II
ASSAY_URL	https://pubs.acs.org/doi/10.1021/es4004153
ASSAY_NOTE	Source: Part II. A temporal study of PFOS and its precursors in human plasma from two German cities in 1982 – 2009; Leo W.Y. Yeung et al.; Sci. Technol. 2013, 47, 8, 3875–3882
ASSAY_NOTE	Data from Supporting Information Table S2. A detailed summary showing the mean PFAS concentrations (ng/mL), standard deviation, range, and number of samples above LOQs in human plasma samples from Münster and Halle.
ASSAY_NOTE	Münster (270 samples) collected; 10 samples per year were analyzed from 1982 to 2009 (except 2006, n = 9), excluding 1994
ASSAY_NOTE	21 PFASs analyzed, 14 reported in Part I; 7 reported in Part II; FOSA was also monitored but was not reported due to poor recovery
ASSAY_NOTE	N for specific year/sex combination not preserved here
ASSAY_NOTE	human plasma samples archived by the German Environmental Specimen Bank (GSB)

ASSAY_NAME	PFAS in plasma from 2 German Cities 1982-2009 (II)
ASSAY_DESCRIPTION	Temporal Study of certain PFAS in archived human plasma from two German cities 1982 – 2009; Part II
ASSAY_URL	https://pubs.acs.org/doi/10.1021/es4004153
ASSAY_NOTE	Source: Part II. A temporal study of PFOS and its precursors in human plasma from two German cities in 1982 – 2009; Leo W.Y. Yeung et al.; Sci. Technol. 2013, 47, 8, 3875–3882
ASSAY_NOTE	Data from Supporting Information Table S2. A detailed summary showing the mean PFAS concentrations (ng/mL), standard deviation, range, and number of samples above LOQs in human plasma samples from Münster and Halle.
ASSAY_NOTE	For Halle (n = 150) (formerly in East Germany), samples were collected annually between 1995 and 2009.
ASSAY_NOTE	21 PFASs analyzed, 14 reported in Part I; 7 reported in Part II; FOSA was also monitored but was not reported due to poor recovery; di-SAmPAPs not analyzed in all samples
ASSAY_NOTE	N for specific year/sex combination not preserved here
ASSAY_NOTE	human plasma samples archived by the German Environmental Specimen Bank (GSB)
